At the interest of protecting commercial interest of members. I suggest we have a SOP'S :standard operating procedures and legal drafts being responsible and esteemed CREA members. 

Lets have 
1.Letter of intent (on letter head) signed by client and service provider (crea member) in two sets of original and once we engage to provide services and end result is the conversion of lead to sale. 

2. MOU : ( On stamp paper) 

These two documents  will broadly covers all terms such as payment or service charges and applicable taxes etc. 
Payment time lines and penalty for delayed payment and protects our interest. 

Before executing the sale deed or lease deed we should sign this or least we do is parallel signing along with transaction  papers like sale deed or lease deed. We insist client to sign our papers too. 

So legally we can fight this out with right legal framework on a given time. It amounts to valid contract and please communicate all through E mail and keep the proof of transactions and communications since these are valid in the court of law. 

This is the basic frame work for  real estate Services  done in USA and UK. 
It's time we standardise our working style.

â€[16/04/18, 4:50:10â€¯PM] CREA (I) MEMBERS: â€image omitted
[16/04/18, 5:54:07â€¯PM] Fransis Crea: Dear CREA (I) Members and Friends

CREA (I) Committee has been debating on an issue highlighted by a few of our very pro-active members, especially engaged in the Primary Markets. 
New Disruptions to Business are a norm and Real Estate Industry will evolve and see a few of them. However, the fundamentals of Business must remain robust and strong to ensure there is a level playing field for all and to this extent CREA (I) has been a torch bearer since its inception.
Exclusive Marketing is not new and not wrong and many of us would do it. Channel Partners and Realtors participating as Consolidators in Exclusive marketing campaign is also perfectly fine. But it is generally done for small to mid-size numbered projects and not for big projects from top banners. Unfortunately, large funded companies are disrupting the markets by engaging in Exclusive Marketing with Top Developers and unfortunately Realtors have been supporting it, more in hunger for business and not visualizing the future.
The database shared is gone forever and the whole branding and marketing effort comes from Realtors like all of us and eventually even though the 2% or more will be paid as commissions, there is an eventual loss of business that is building up. The trust is higher on platforms of Associations as there are no personal interests involved and hence CREA (I) would like to deal directly with Developers for all its Members and not through exclusively assigned largely funded companies that are cornering the market share that will hurt everyoneâ€™s interest, not in the long run but very shortly itself.
In lieu of this discussion, CREA (I) Committee has decided to request all its members NOT TO ATTEND the Salarpuria East Crest Launch Event today, organized by one such company that is taking massive exclusive mandates banking on the strength of Individual Realtors like you. We would instead let the Developers know that we would prefer to market directly under the CREA (I) umbrella and that will ensure better commissions, smoother interactions and faster payments with no false promises as you all have experienced over last many years.
PLEASE ENSURE NO CREA (I) Member attends todayâ€™s planned launch Event.
Best Wishes
CREA (I) Committee
